Hi Michael,
I see EID 108821456, Amt $477.00 item was released from user hold successfully by the user the Nlim at 03/16/2022 17:41:42. 
when the user was trying to release  EID 109164531, Amt $.34 item the user encountered severe constraint error on database processing 
and user's GUI database session closed. when user tried to release item again user encountered oracle connection error that is expected. 
when Rsantamari tried from different database session it had been released successfully at .

"Severe constraint error" is caused by exceptional situation occurred on the database while processing constraints. 
this possible at lower level. In this case client need to close GUI as mentioned in the popup error message. 
Reopening GUI and retrying same action will work.

Will this change be implemented during an accepted change window for the target service(s)? Yes -- Answer should be 'No'

So, please cancel the task - CHT22002350191 created for backout. Only allowing the time equal to backout duration at the end of last task suffices.

CH22000926689  - 


301 - CH21000706946

1. Java change ticket - Rejected. (ref old ticket 301 - CH21000706946)

1) Although Risk Assessment states "no customer affecting service outage" for this activity as scheduled, the Change Plan documents an application or server restart, therefore a corresponding Outage Record is required for ALL Affected CIs so that comprehensive Conflict Analysis can be performed against other changes in this same window. Please use the Additional Actions menu in upper left of grey header (3 lines/hamburger) to Create Outage record

2) Change Justification question is specific to BUSINESS Validation "[If a "Business Verification" task is not required, please provide the reason] Validation task required, Already added validation task --------> there is No Business Validation Task included; why is there no Business Validation necessary? If required, it should describe the low level technical details as how the business will verify the change.

3) Change Window must allow for potential Backout. Verification Tasks last through to the end of the Change Window and do not allow for a possible rollback within the window (mandatory audit item). The overall change window must account for the backout duration too, therefore tasks must be planned accordingly and not make up the entirety of the change window, to accommodate the time needed for a backout.

4) The Task Types are not accurate to the nature of the activity described: for example, the Bit9 Unlock task should be listed as Pre Implementation task, etc. Validation tasks should not include steps of deployment or implementation

create or replace 
PROCEDURE             SENDMAILWEB (
out_err_id OUT NUMBER,
out_err_msg OUT VARCHAR2,
msg_text varchar2,
mailhost VARCHAR2,
msg_from varchar2,
msg_to varchar2,
msg_subject varchar2
)
IS
    l_boundary      varchar2(255) default 'a1b2c3d4e3f2g1';
    l_body_html     clob := empty_clob;  --This LOB will be the email message
    l_offset        number;
    l_ammount       number;
    l_temp          varchar2(32767) default null;
    l_server	    VARCHAR2(35);
    source_ip       VARCHAR2(15);
    msg_data        varchar2(32767) default null;
    l_vrfy_msg    utl_smtp.reply;
c utl_smtp.connection;
rc integer;
--msg_to varchar2(40) : =anand.kumar.sivakumar@fnis.com;
--msg_subject varchar2(50) :=Testing;
--msg_text varchar2(50) :=forward;
BEGIN
	out_err_id := 0;
  

    IF mailhost IS NULL THEN
      l_server := 'smtprelay.messageprovider.com'; --10.0.33.36
    ELSE
    	l_server := 'smtprelay.messageprovider.com';
    END IF;

-- R120414623 Naresh-- Changed to pick the server IP from achps_const table START

 SELECT  trim(parameter_name) 
	INTO   source_ip
	FROM   achps_const
	WHERE  rec_id = 'EMAIL' and rownum = 1;

-- R120414623 Naresh-- Changed to pick the server IP from achps_const table END

c := utl_smtp.open_connection(l_server, 25); -- SMTP on port 25
utl_smtp.helo(c, source_ip);

--Koti, Start here
--l_vrfy_msg := UTL_SMTP.VRFY( c, msg_to );
--dbms_output.put_line(l_vrfy_msg.code);
--IF l_vrfy_msg.code = 550 THEN
--              RAISE_APPLICATION_ERROR (-20001,'Invalid recipient address');
--END IF;
--Koti, End here

utl_smtp.mail(c, msg_from);
utl_smtp.rcpt(c, msg_to);

--utl_smtp.data(c,'From: '||msg_from || utl_tcp.crlf ||
--'To: ' || msg_to || utl_tcp.crlf ||
--'Subject: ' || msg_subject ||
--utl_tcp.crlf);


    l_temp := l_temp || 'MIME-Version: 1.0' ||  chr(13) || chr(10);
    l_temp := l_temp || 'To: ' || msg_to || chr(13) || chr(10);
    l_temp := l_temp || 'From: ' || msg_from || chr(13) || chr(10);
    l_temp := l_temp || 'Subject: ' || msg_subject || chr(13) || chr(10);
    l_temp := l_temp || 'Reply-To: ' || msg_from ||  chr(13) || chr(10);
    l_temp := l_temp || 'Content-Type: multipart/alternative; boundary=' ||
                         chr(34) || l_boundary ||  chr(34) || chr(13) ||
                         chr(10);
    ----------------------------------------------------
    -- Write the headers
    dbms_lob.createtemporary( l_body_html, false, 10 );
    dbms_lob.write(l_body_html,length(l_temp),1,l_temp);
    ----------------------------------------------------
    -- Write the text boundary
    l_offset := dbms_lob.getlength(l_body_html) + 1;
    l_temp   := '--' || l_boundary || chr(13)||chr(10);
    l_temp   := l_temp || 'content-type: text/plain; charset=us-ascii' ||
                  chr(13) || chr(10) || chr(13) || chr(10);
    dbms_lob.write(l_body_html,length(l_temp),l_offset,l_temp);
    ----------------------------------------------------
    -- Write the plain text portion of the email
    l_offset := dbms_lob.getlength(l_body_html) + 1;
   -- dbms_lob.write(l_body_html,length(p_text),l_offset,p_text);
    ----------------------------------------------------
    -- Write the HTML boundary
    l_temp   := chr(13)||chr(10)||chr(13)||chr(10)||'--' || l_boundary ||
                    chr(13) || chr(10);
    l_temp   := l_temp || 'content-type: text/html;' ||
                   chr(13) || chr(10) || chr(13) || chr(10);
    l_offset := dbms_lob.getlength(l_body_html) + 1;
    dbms_lob.write(l_body_html,length(l_temp),l_offset,l_temp);
    ----------------------------------------------------
    -- Write the HTML portion of the message
    l_offset := dbms_lob.getlength(l_body_html) + 1;
    dbms_lob.write(l_body_html,length(msg_text),l_offset,msg_text);
    ----------------------------------------------------
    -- Write the final html boundary
    l_temp   := chr(13) || chr(10) || '--' ||  l_boundary || '--' || chr(13);
    l_offset := dbms_lob.getlength(l_body_html) + 1;
    dbms_lob.write(l_body_html,length(l_temp),l_offset,l_temp);
    ----------------------------------------------------
    -- Send the email in 1900 byte chunks to UTL_SMTP
    l_offset  := 1;
    l_ammount := 1900;
    utl_smtp.open_data(c);
    while l_offset < dbms_lob.getlength(l_body_html) loop

        msg_data := dbms_lob.substr(l_body_html,l_ammount,l_offset);
        utl_smtp.write_data(c,
                            dbms_lob.substr(l_body_html,l_ammount,l_offset));
        l_offset  := l_offset + l_ammount ;
        l_ammount := least(1900,dbms_lob.getlength(l_body_html) - l_ammount);
    end loop;
    utl_smtp.close_data(c);
    utl_smtp.quit(c);
    dbms_lob.freetemporary(l_body_html);
    out_err_msg := 0;




--utl_smtp.quit(c);
EXCEPTION
WHEN UTL_SMTP.INVALID_OPERATION THEN
        dbms_output.put_line(' Invalid Operation in Mail attemptusing UTL_SMTP.');
        out_err_id := SQLCODE;
        out_err_msg := SUBSTR(SQLERRM, 1, 100);

WHEN UTL_SMTP.TRANSIENT_ERROR THEN
        dbms_output.put_line(' Temporary e-mail issue - try again');
        out_err_id := SQLCODE;
        out_err_msg := SUBSTR(SQLERRM, 1, 100);

WHEN UTL_SMTP.PERMANENT_ERROR THEN
        dbms_output.put_line(' Permanent Error Encountered.');
        out_err_id := SQLCODE;
        out_err_msg := SUBSTR(SQLERRM, 1, 100);

WHEN OTHERS THEN
        out_err_id := SQLCODE;
        out_err_msg := SUBSTR(SQLERRM, 1, 100);
        return;

END;
-----------------------------------------------END-OF-DAY-----------------------------------------------

IN21005259004  opened by City National Bank

Root Cause:
For Delivery Endpoints with Delivery Vehicle=E-mail, a user is unable to save an email address containing a & character in the email name. Email address can contain a & character, therefore, logic needs to be modified to allow the character when saving an email address.

Justification:
This impedes the users ability to setup valid email addresses within ACHPS for corporate reporting.  Without the ability to establish an email address, the bank must resort to using Delivery Vehicle=Fax to have reports faxed to the corporate client.  Fax is not business standard for the bank.  

-----------------------------------------------END-OF-DAY-----------------------------------------------

select sum(txn_count)/sum(minutes) txn_per_min
From (SELECT 
fc.file_name,
fc.original_entry_addn_cnt txn_count,
(TO_DATE(to_char(fc.achin_end_ts, 'dd/mm/yyyy HH24:MI:SS'),'dd/mm/yyyy HH24:MI:SS')-TO_DATE(to_char(fc.achin_beg_ts, 'dd/mm/yyyy HH24:MI:SS'),'dd/mm/yyyy HH24:MI:SS')) * 24 * 60 minutes
FROM FILE_CNTL fc, 
     file_id fid 
where fc.fi_rt='211590671' 
and fc.fi_rt=fid.fi_rt 
and fc.file_id=fid.file_id
and fc.inbound_file_yn='Y' 
and fc.imm_origin_name<>'GENERATED RETURNS' 
and fid.foreign_orig_yn='Y');

script
-------

set serveroutput on

declare
TYPE fi_rt_t IS TABLE OF fi.fi_rt%TYPE INDEX BY PLS_INTEGER;
all_fi_rt fi_rt_t;
min_txn_per_min number(10);
max_txn_per_min number(10);

begin

     SELECT fi_rt BULK COLLECT INTO all_fi_rt FROM fi;

     FOR indx IN 1 .. all_fi_rt.COUNT
     LOOP
        select min(original_entry_addn_cnt/ minutes), max(original_entry_addn_cnt/ minutes) 
        into min_txn_per_min, max_txn_per_min
        from 
          (select file_name,file_creat_ts,recv_file_ts,imm_dst,imm_origin,achin_beg_ts,achin_end_ts,original_batch_cnt,original_entry_addn_cnt,
          (TO_DATE(to_char(achin_end_ts, 'dd/mm/yyyy HH24:MI:SS'),'dd/mm/yyyy HH24:MI:SS')-TO_DATE(to_char(achin_beg_ts, 'dd/mm/yyyy HH24:MI:SS'),'dd/mm/yyyy HH24:MI:SS')) * 24 * 60 minutes
          from file_cntl 
          where fi_rt=all_fi_rt (indx) 
          and inbound_file_yn='Y') 
        where minutes>=1;
        
        dbms_output.put_line(all_fi_rt (indx) || ' '|| min_txn_per_min || ' ' ||  max_txn_per_min );
     END LOOP;

end;
/

SELECT  f.fi_rt, f.file_cntl_id, f.integ_ck_yn, 
			sum(batch_cnt) batch_count,
			sum(dist_cr_entry_cnt + dist_db_entry_cnt + non_dist_cr_entry_cnt + non_dist_db_entry_cnt ) entry_count
			FROM file_cntl f
			WHERE f.fi_rt ='122104813'			
			AND (
			 (f.file_status = 'D' 
			  AND to_char(f.all_batch_dist_ts,'YYYYMMDD') < to_char(sysdate-90,'YYYYMMDD')
			and f.inbound_file_yn = 'Y') 
			 OR 
			  ( file_status IN ('L', 'P', 'R', 'S') 
			  AND to_char(recv_file_ts,'YYYYMMDD') < to_char(sysdate-90,'YYYYMMDD')) 
			 OR 
			(file_status = 'D' 
			   AND to_char(all_batch_dist_ts,'YYYYMMDD') < to_char(sysdate-90,'YYYYMMDD')			
			AND inbound_file_yn = 'N')
			)
			AND f.integ_ck_yn = 'N'
			group by f.fi_rt, f.file_cntl_id, f.file_name, f.integ_ck_yn 
			order by entry_count desc;

select job_machine,
       no,
	     substr(command_line,instr(command_line,'FI_RT=')+6,10),
       j_name,step,
       s_name,
       date_time_started,
       date_time_completed,
       command_line 
from stepq
where status='A' 
and date_time_started is not null
and trunc(date_time_started)=trunc(sysdate)
and job_machine in (select proc_name from pq where job_num>0)
order by date_time_started;

SELECT 
		file_cntl_id,
 	    TO_string(recv_file_ts, 'YYYYMMDD HH24MI'),
        TO_string(all_batch_dist_ts, 'MM/DD/YYYY'),
		risk_db_entry_cnt,
		risk_cr_entry_cnt,
		risk_tot_db_entry_amt,
		risk_tot_cr_entry_amt,
		dist_db_entry_cnt,
		dist_cr_entry_cnt,
		dist_tot_db_entry_amt, 
		dist_tot_cr_entry_amt, 
		non_dist_db_entry_cnt,
		non_dist_cr_entry_cnt,
		non_dist_tot_db_entry_amt, 
		non_dist_tot_cr_entry_amt, 
 		file_status,
	    imm_origin_name,
	    stl_db_entry_cnt,
	    stl_cr_entry_cnt,
		stl_tot_db_entry_amt, 
		stl_tot_cr_entry_amt
	FROM  file_cntl
	WHERE fi_rt = '273970116'
	AND  inbound_file_yn = 'Y'
	AND (file_status in ('A','H')
         OR (file_status ='D' and TO_string(all_batch_dist_ts,'MM/DD/YYYY') = '10/05/2020')
         OR (file_status in ('P', 'S', 'R') and TO_string(achin_end_ts,'MM/DD/YYYY') = '10/05/2020'))
ORDER BY file_cntl_id;

--and bc.file_cntl_id=o.file_cntl_id
--and bc.batch_cntl_id=o.batch_cntl_id
and bc.sec_code='ARC'
and o.ret_chg_reason_code='R38';
